Giving to the Poor 219

— Meng Xiao

The northwest wind is blowing with a sting. Little Sanzi is only wearing a tattered lined jacket, but he is anxiously looking... the ground is covered with a few inches of thick snow. Little Sanzi got up early and put the empty iron can on his wrist, hurrying towards the soup kitchen.

"If I had a silver dollar, I wouldn't die..." Little Sanzi mumbled, spitting hard and cursing, "Damn it, these kids, there's no law!"

His broken boots squeaked on the snow. Some of the snow had already been trampled solid, and his feet slipped as he stepped down. Little Sanzi ran for a while and felt a little tired. His stomach was also rumbling. He hadn't eaten all day, no wonder he felt weak. He thought to himself:

"Alas, every year is worse than the last. Last year in the Northeast, it didn't matter if I went hungry for three or two days. Now, my body is getting worse and worse. After being hungry for a day, it's like a smoker who hasn't had enough opium, I don't have the strength to do anything." He shook his head, and the snowflakes on the edge of his broken felt hat fell on his shoulders.

As Little Sanzi walked, he thought about those golden days when he was in the Northeast. Although he wasn't enjoying leisure, he had food and clothing. Like now, it's December, and there's a small western-style stove at home. As long as there are a few small coal balls, the room is very warm. In the evening, he might even go to Zhang Erzi's place to buy two ounces of white liquor and drink it slowly...

"Damn it, ×× people!" Little Sanzi cursed fiercely, suddenly feeling a little dizzy. He was too agitated.

"Son of a bitch, these bastards, made me suffer the insolence of those kids in the soup kitchen today?" With that, Little Sanzi thought of what had happened at the soup kitchen. "Those kids throwing their weight around, acting like officials, damn it ×, one day..." Little Sanzi's heart was on fire, and he accelerated his pace, as if his empty stomach was filled with anger.

There were more and more pedestrians on the road, and the trams were also leaving the factory. A child selling fried dough sticks darted out of an alley, shouting loudly.

"Third Brother, good morning! Going to the factory in Ximen?" The child selling fried dough sticks greeted him.

"Yes, are you going too?"

"Later, the factory doesn't open until 7:30! I'll just be drinking the northwest wind at the factory gate if I go too early!" The child walked away. Little Sanzi thought to himself, if I had some acquaintances or a little capital, it would be good to sell fried dough sticks. With my good hands and feet, I'm competing with those old men and women for this bowl of porridge. It's really--no progress!

He had already reached the edge of Xizhimen City, and a gust of north wind blew him back two or three steps. What a strong wind! Little Sanzi shivered and hurriedly tightened his collar, walking at an angle.

There were a few people on the road, also wearing broken tin cans on their wrists, some supporting the old and some pulling the young. They were going to the soup kitchen together. Little Sanzi looked at them and felt even more uncomfortable. He cursed himself:

"Competing with these old people and women for this meal is really too cruel--sin, sin!" Just as Little Sanzi thought this, another thought immediately refuted him: "What's the matter? Don't you have any capital? You have..."

He arrived at the soup kitchen. A decent-looking policeman was waving a stick, telling them to line up: "Whoever comes first, goes in first, don't push, don't shout! You must maintain--order!"

"What an act!" Little Sanzi looked down on these people. He muttered to himself.

"Officer, I can't walk anymore, please be lenient!" An old woman sat on the snow, begging the policeman.

"No! You have to line up. You can't go in if you don't line up!" He pointed at the old woman with his stick, shouting with a thick neck.

"Ouch--!" The old woman just climbed up and fell down again, lying on the ground, wailing.

"These bastards, putting on airs." Little Sanzi thought, just as he was about to go over, someone had already helped the old woman up.

"I can't stand up! My legs can't take it, you... Ouch--!" the old woman said, the tin can hanging on her wrist fell to the ground, tumbling and clattering, falling below the small pile of soil.

The door of the soup kitchen opened. Standing outside, you could see several large pots steaming with white smoke. Little Sanzi seemed to smell the fragrance of millet, and his saliva dripped uncontrollably. He waited anxiously, his stomach rumbling even more fiercely.

"Two and a half portions per person, yesterday there were still three." A young woman ran out, complaining unintentionally. "There's not even black beans left, just chaff."

When it was Little Sanzi's turn, he held up his tin can. He looked at the man holding the ladle with greedy eyes.

"You fix it, then give me half a portion!"

"Two portions per person, no one can have more!"

"They all had two and a half portions, why do I have two portions? We have to be reasonable, don't make a fuss!"

"Get out of here! Who's taking your money, owing you, selling to you?"

Little Sanzi turned around, muttering: "Listen, women get two and a half portions, we're not tender-skinned, so we get half a portion less! It's not like he's taking the money out of his own pocket, and he's still trying to take credit!"

"What are you shouting about! Take him to the police station, a lawless bastard!"

A black hand grabbed the back of Little Sanzi's head, and another hand grabbed Little Sanzi's arm. His tin can fell to the ground, some yellow rice porridge splashing on the snow, steaming.

Poverty 220

— Man Yin

I have always been content with poverty, and I have never had a moment's fantasy about the luxury and wealth of others swirling in my mind. As a person, as long as you are true to your own conscience, what does the emperor's power have to do with me? That's how I've lived my life until now. This summer, trying to help a friend, we both ended up losing our jobs. My friend repeatedly apologized to me, but since I could live with my conscience, I didn't resent anyone. But confined to my cramped attic room every day, I began to feel uneasy about poverty. My temper suddenly flared up, and I learned to scold people, even someone I had no connection with. Sometimes I would throw things, things I had bought with the price of my labor. I couldn't stand the pressure of over a hundred degrees. That old woman said I couldn't stand the threat of hunger, and to be content with poverty, you at least had to be able to fill your stomach. I began to understand how lotteries, gambling, and all the sins that the law doesn't allow come about. At that time, although I was no longer content with poverty, I hadn't yet crossed the line. When I found another job, I was content with poverty as usual. I was satisfied.

In my current job, the work is more demanding than before, but the pay is less than half of what it used to be. I've been in this job for nearly three months, and I'm doing my work with a clear conscience. I don't envy those who are "lying on firewood and tasting gall." Recently, the north wind has been howling, and the grass and trees are withering. Every night when I return home from work, my thin clothes can't withstand the cold wind. Often, when I'm walking slowly on the side of the road instead of taking a car, I can't help but glance at those people in heavy fur coats, and I silently think that they probably don't feel the terror of winter. When these thoughts invade my mind, I know that I'm starting to become dissatisfied with my life again. To do things with a clear conscience and be content with poverty, there's also the condition of protecting body temperature besides filling your stomach.

These days, I can't help but become lazy at work, hoping to see if those who are well-fed and warmly clothed might bestow a bit of unexpected sympathy. But nothing happens. They immediately feel that the price they paid isn't yielding the expected results and become angry. I'm scolded by those people like a pig or a dog. On the way home, I think about committing sins that go beyond the pale, planning how to retaliate against those people, or how to acquire an unexpected sum of money so I can join their ranks and show them off. As I'm walking along, thinking about this, on the side of a department store, I'm blocked by a group of vagrants. When I try to turn around and take another road, a police officer suddenly appears and takes the vagrants away. From the passersby's discussion, I learn that those vagrants were抢奪搶奪搶奪搶奪 the department store's sidewalk space. Because there's a generator in the department store's basement, the electricity spreads along the sidewalk, making even the cement unusually warm, and those vagrants wanted to抢奪抢奪 it as a place to avoid the cold for the night. I'm moved by this scene. I should focus on my work. I'm not the poorest person in the world. Perhaps there are thousands upon thousands of hands trying to seize my job, and thousands upon thousands of eyes envying my thin cotton clothes. (One of the winter night essays)

Opening Introduction 221

Daiyu Laments Autumn

Sad flowers, sad grass, a dreary sky. A chilling wind and rain beat against the window curtains. A thousand emerald bamboos rustle in the wind. A garden of fragrant grass is covered in drizzling rain. In the Xiaoxiang Pavilion, silence reigns. The flower-burying maiden is listless with illness. Thinking of her, she is full of sorrow, sickness, and even more resentment. Lamentable, singable, and pitiable. Her face is even thinner than a plum blossom. Her delicate breaths are as thin as a wisp of smoke. She is a sickly Xishi, unable to withstand the wind. A sorrowful Xi Gui remains silent. All day long, she dabs at the grease marks on her face and washes away tears. The medicine furnace and tea stove are steeped in sorrow. All one sees is that the prescription on the desk is a foot thick. The mirror on the dressing table lacks luster. Look at her, sitting listlessly, abandoning her toilette, weary of sleep. In her sorrow, she divines her heart's affairs in dreams. She barely manages to tidy the snow-white hair at her temples. The pearly tears well up like a spring. She languidly rises from the bed after knocking the red beans to pieces. She wearily goes to sleep late at night after picking out the wick of the green lamp. The plum blossom paper tent fails to conjure a dream. The lotus-silk embroidered quilt is half-cast aside. Deep in autumn, she still wears her gossamer-thin garments. Fresh tears still cling to the green gauze curtain. Zijuan wipes away tears as she attends to the tea caddy. Xueyan grieves as she tends to the smoke from the medicine. All one hears are her constant coughs and sighs. She clutches her intestines and weeps silently. She says, "Zijuan, people say that autumn is a time for enjoying the scenery. Why is it that when I, your mistress, see autumn, my sorrow only increases? Look at that autumn moon, hazy and cold as water. The autumn wind is rustling and cold as scissors. The autumn light flows like the wanderer's journey, the autumn rain drips, stirring thoughts of autumn. The autumn insects chirp, wanting to break the soul. Although autumn is just beginning, my dreams are already chaotic and disordered. The autumn mountains are silent, luring travelers to become drunk. The autumn waves roll, urging guests to return home. So much of the autumn scenery is distressing. That is why I, your mistress, cannot bear to mention the word 'autumn.' Alas, I, your mistress, am far from my homeland, thousands of miles away. My drifting existence is here. I crane my neck, but cannot see my homeland. Lonely and bitter, like a lone goose. Planning to rebel against my family and country is like a pie in the sky. I fear that returning to my old home will become an empty promise. I imagine that a lump of yellow earth will be in a desolate place. My withered bones will be buried in a foreign land. Moreover, my parents have already withered like autumn leaves. Why should a crabapple bloom brightly in the sun? When sorrow gathers, the nights seem like years. When sickness comes, the autumn months seem like years. I think back and forth about the three autumns of a single day. The five winds and ten waves make for thousands of miles. My intestines twist nine times, and my heart is quiet. I hate to declare the three stacks of Yangguan Pass. I only fear that medicine will be unable to cure my illness. It will only be that time passes in vain, a fleeting life. That is why I, your mistress, will not open my mirror case when I am about to die. I vow never to wear gold ornaments again. I, your mistress, always spend my youthful days in sorrow. I entrust my every thought to my sorrowful spirit. I, your mistress, have treated a fickle man as a passionate lover. Who knows that the Tushita Heaven is actually the Heaven of Departure and Hatred? To this day, good things vaguely become illusory dreams. The warmth and coldness of human relationships have all changed like mulberry fields. Soft words and gentle speech are all false. How can there be eternity? All of this is because I am willingly taking on suffering because of my karma. I am binding myself like a stiff silkworm, using rushes to punish myself. Is it not true that I am grieving from the bottom of my heart, pursuing the past without limit? My firm will to repent has already turned into a spring. Alas, I, your mistress, am sick and dying, and no one asks after me. I lie on my bed, and who pities me? Alas, I, your mistress, secretly sheds tears under the rain-drenched lotus leaves. The dewdrops on the lotus pods are a field of bitter hearts. Alas, I, your mistress, sees no one's shadow offering comfort at my bedside. Only illness comes to my pillow. Alas, I, your mistress, has no interest in reciting poetry. I have no inclination to play the zither. Alas, I, your mistress, the inkstone pool has long been dry and teeming with 鱓魚. I cannot bear to continue writing the poem about burying flowers. I am most afraid to hear the cuckoo singing on the branches, startling my good dreams. I am most afraid of the parrot in front of the window learning my words. I am most afraid to hear the wind tinkling the iron horse bells, clear as speech. The rain sprinkles the cold window, thin as smoke. That Lady Lin cannot bear the joy of autumn. It is pitiful, one drop of blood and tears, one word of lament. I wonder why He Zhi is so ill-fated. Why is writing talent forbidden for beautiful women? I want to loudly question the heavens in the sky."

Storytelling 224

Xia Hesheng's Three Smiles

Dun Ben (800) 7:00 PM to 8:00 PM

Opening: "Beheading Han Xin"

Ke Han was Han Xin in those years. He was, in essence, a struggling person wandering the streets. At that time, he hadn't met the true lord destined by Heaven. It was as if a dragon was trapped in the water, suffering hardship. He once met a prostitute who washed silk floss for him. He received a deep kindness from a beggar who gave him a meal. Later, he repaid the kindness with a thousand gold pieces. He was, a poor man standing on the street with an empty purse. He carried a dragon spring sword on his back. He ignored the taunts of the butcher's son. He ignored the shame of enduring humiliation under the crotch. He abandoned his pen and joined the Han army. But alas, he was full of strategies but hadn't met his opportunity. It was all because he accidentally boasted of his great ambitions after getting drunk. He almost suffered torture at the city execution grounds. Therefore, he secretly fled at night. Xiao He chased Han Xin under the moon. Golden words of advice from the Han ruler protected him. He ascended the altar and was appointed a great general. The sound of the wind and the cries of the cranes chronicled his achievements. The two heroes, Chu and Han, fought fiercely. Han Xin was, like a bamboo splitting, defeating the Overlord. His strategies wiped out the Xiang army. It was all because of his great efforts and hard work. He was made the King of Chu and stationed in Huaiyin. Once suspected, he was lured in. His title was stripped, and he was made a Marquis, his command of troops was taken away. It was all because the Han Emperor was indulging in pleasures in the palace. He enjoyed the warmth and joy of rewarding beauties. He indulged in dreams of butterflies and pursued pleasure. He ignored the grand court of the magnificent empire. Therefore, Han Xin secretly rebelled in Huaiyin. How could he know that Lu Zhi would lure him into the palace? Alas, he was murdered in the bell chamber. The good bow is hidden when the flying bird is gone. Once achievements turn into a painted cake.

Shen Bao Local Supplement Automobile Weekly

The American Automobile Industry is Gradually Recovering and Prospering 231

— Yu

Manufacturers Implement New Cooperation Plans—Reasons for Advancing the Date of the Annual Auto Show

The automobile business in the United States, after several years of hard work, is now gradually moving towards improvement. Just like American Automobile Manufacturers Association Chairman Alvin Macauley likened it, he said in essence that the current automobile manufacturing industry is like playing soccer. After everyone's communication work, the ball has been repeatedly obtained by us. Continuing to use the communication method, the obtained ball is kicked to the enemy's position. After such a reversal of danger, the spirit of the players is refreshed, everyone is particularly excited, and they have the courage to win outwards.

The above-mentioned determination to win is now buried in the hearts of the leaders of the automobile manufacturing industry. Since they won the ball back in 1932, they have been working hard and doing a good job of communication. The ball is often placed under their jurisdiction and passes the middle line, shooting directly on the road to recovery and prosperity. Car manufacturers are now using a good strategy, that is, in terms of product, constantly striving for perfection, so that the value of the car exceeds the price paid by the customers. This is the most effective and always good strategy in an invincible place.

Taking the facts, the amount of cars produced this year really matches the metaphor cited above. According to the forecast, the production of automobiles and commercial trucks in the United States this year will be about three, six hundred and seventy-five thousand vehicles. This number not only exceeds last year's output by 28%, but also increases by about two and a half times compared with the production in 1932. According to the available figures, the retail sales in the domestic market in 1935 were 38% higher than last year. More than 40% for passenger cars, and more than 30% for trucks. Calculated on Labor Day, the number of retail cars this year has exceeded the total sales in the twelve months of 1932.

Speaking of foreign sales, because of the increasing needs of the world, it is expected that the total number of exported cars in 1935 will reach 535,000, an increase of 27% compared to last year. There are more than one reasons why foreign trade can improve so much. The most obvious is the stability of foreign exchange, the establishment of reciprocal tariffs between countries, and the gradual recovery of prosperity in major countries, and the increase in the value of American-made cars, etc. All have a related relationship.

The debut of the new autumn model car is even more helpful for foreign sales. American-made cars were marketed to the Southern Hemisphere for the first time this year. When their important sales season begins, new cars can be sold in a timely manner. When the European Auto Show is held, American-made European cars will also be offered at the same time. The number of American shipments to the Southern Hemisphere has increased significantly in the past two years. New cars will continue to be exported next spring. It is predicted that about 60% of the total exports will be sold there.

The number of new 1936 cars that can be sold abroad should be around 650,000. In this way, workers will benefit greatly in terms of obtaining work, whether directly or indirectly. It is estimated that 125,000 people will get jobs in the car manufacturing, parts, tires, and other related industries. It has to be said that it is a great help. There is also a more solemn estimate that the number of new 1936 cars sold abroad is roughly 635,000.

Recently, American car manufacturers have implemented a very good spirit of cooperation to stabilize car production. This plan has started this year. One end of this plan is to hold the annual car exhibition two months earlier. It opened in New York in November this year. The overall main purpose of the cooperation plan is to make the work of the automobile manufacturing industry and its related industries to be evenly distributed, and not to reduce work in the slack seasons.

The main significance of this cooperation plan can be observed from various facts. Usually, the number of car sales fluctuates due to seasonal reasons, causing the production volume to sometimes be high and sometimes low, and the work of the workers is greatly affected. Sometimes the production volume in slack months is 30% lower than that of busy months. Because the normal production volume cannot be maintained in winter in preparation for spring sales, the work that workers have obtained at this time in previous years is relatively limited.

In order to solve this problem and improve the working conditions of workers, the manufacturers have started an ambitious plan this year. One of the features is to advance the annual car exhibition, which was held in January in the past, to mid-November. In the past thirty years, the auto show has been opened in January as usual. In addition, the manufacturers have also agreed to adopt a new plan in terms of ordering raw materials, so that workers in various industries related to automobiles can obtain the greatest work benefits. On the one hand, it allows the automobile manufacturers' own workers to obtain full work in January and February, manufacturing various new car parts that will be launched in the spring.

In the past two months, other important industries in the United States have also adopted a drastic change. The tightening that was implemented from autumn to autumn has now changed its policy. Because since September, it has been felt that there is a need to increase. For example, the steel industry has more than doubled compared to the same period in the past. Other railways, mining, etc. also have the same phenomenon. As for the various large and small industries related to renting car manufacturing, it goes without saying.

If you want to make the above plan a success, then there are two major points that cannot be ignored. First, the number of retail sales in winter must increase. Second, the current spirit of cooperation between labor and management must be well maintained. The sales of sedans in the car market are getting better year by year. Because the manufacturers' production, sedan-style cars account for 99% of the total. And modern roads can enable vehicles to drive in all seasons. For these two reasons, the car sales this winter are expected to be very impressive.

Another Ironclad Proof of the Safety and Reliability of the New Dodge Automobile 232

— Yun

Those who have visited the Dodge inspection grounds, upon witnessing the various rigorous tests to which Dodge automobiles are subjected, almost invariably shake their heads and sigh, believing that the tests performed on the Dodge by the inspection machines are exceedingly cruel. However, from another perspective, these rigorous tests are actually an expression of humanitarianism and can by no means be considered cruel. The sole purpose of the inspection is to use experimental methods to definitively prove the safety and reliability of driving.

According to Dodge engineers, this type of inspection machine is called the "Belgian Roll." One day of testing a Dodge automobile on this machine is equivalent to the wear and tear it would experience in several years of arduous service under ideal conditions. Therefore, any minor flaws are bound to be discovered immediately and cannot be concealed. If it were for daily driving, such minor defects would never be noticed even after years. The Dodge automobile is uniquely able to successfully handle these absolutely rigorous and uncompromising tests, proving that its chassis, body, engine, wheels, and all other parts of the car are perfect, and that its driving safety and reliability have been further proven.

The above is a heroic image of the new Dodge six-cylinder two-door convertible. 233

The Function of the Newly Invented Flag Brand Bosch Battery Charger 234

— Fu

At a time when coil ignition is most widely used and the types of electrical parts on automobiles are increasing daily, the most necessary and indispensable item is the storage battery. If the storage battery can fully exert its effectiveness without any shortcomings, then even in extremely difficult and challenging situations, it can be easily managed and overcome. All of these situations are well known to those in the automotive industry who have experience. Since the function of the storage battery is so extensive and important, the invention of the new Flag Brand Bosch charger has great value and an important contribution that goes without saying.

The Flag Brand Bosch charger is a truly economical and cost-effective new invention. Using this device to charge the battery overnight will naturally ensure that the battery has ample power. Therefore, driving the car the next morning will start instantly and respond immediately. The lifespan of the storage battery itself is also extended as a result. Furthermore, what is especially commendable is that this device can fully charge the battery in two nights without any risk of overcharging. When the battery reaches its maximum capacity, the charging rate automatically reduces to a trickle, causing no damage to the battery.

It is said that this charger is of no small benefit to car owners who have car radios, as it can be used to make the radio's sound extremely clear and pleasant. As for families who only use their cars on weekends, they only need to purchase one of these chargers to completely solve the problem of weekly battery charging and save a lot of trouble. Moreover, this charger is not only suitable for car owners but also needed by doctors, wholesale merchants, laundry workers, bakers, collectors, department stores, etc. This device comes in two styles for use with large and small batteries. The electricity it uses is similar to that of a medium-sized light bulb, making it very economical.

General Situation of Guangxi Highways 235

— Yong

Second Year Construction Routes

(1) Complete the Limeng Road. The roadbed of this road, which starts from Zhangcun, east of Lipu city, to Duying in Mengshan, a distance of 25 li, has long been completed. The roadbed from Duying to Mao'ertang, a distance of 27 li, and the bridge and culvert projects are not very large. However, the section from Mengshan city, passing through Shuidou, crossing Xinkai Datang,绕 Bai Zhulong, passing Xiaoshuiyong, and reaching Chencun, and then from Chencun, passing through Junchang,绕 Shangtiangang, crossing Pingdongyong, and reaching Taiping, is 140 li long. The road work is relatively large, and there are many bridges and culverts. The section from Taiping to Mengjiang has been open to traffic for a long time and does not require further construction. The distance from Lipu to Liuguihe and other places is similar. If the entire Limeng line is open to traffic, the traffic between the Gui area and the Wuzhou River will be very convenient. Even the passenger and cargo traffic in the Liuzhou area along the Liujiang River can繞 Lipu to reach Mengjiang and the Wuzhou River. Not only can the traffic between Gui and Wu, and Liu and Wu, be achieved in one day, but also passengers from Guilin, Liuzhou and He can take a boat upstream after arriving in Mengjiang, passing through Wulin along the Rongwu Road to Rongxian, and reaching Yulin. With the road circulating smoothly, the Limeng line can not only directly connect the highways of the Liuzhou and Guilin areas to the big river, but also connect the routes of the Liuzhou, Guilin, and Wuzhou areas with each other. The relationship is very important for internal transportation. It was originally planned to be built at the same time as the first-year lines, but since the first year required more than two million yuan, adding this line would place an excessive burden on the treasury. Therefore, it was decided to complete this line in the second year after the completion of the first-year lines.

Third Year Construction Routes

(1) Build the Jiuda Road. This road starts from Jiudunxu in Du'an, passing through Tiantacun, Lantang, Wengdong, Yaonan, Lizi, Xia'ao, Guangjiong, to Naling. It is mostly rugged and winding, with towering cliffs and strange rocks overlapping each other. The engineering is very large. The section from Naling via Baoping to Jiuxu is relatively straight. The section from Jiuxu via Changzhi to Dachang is difficult to determine. The entire line is more than 200 li long. After the completion of this road, the route from Qinzhou Haikou via Nanning, Wuming, Du'an, Chehe, to Liuzhai in Qian, compared to the route via Sa迁, Daqing, Hechi to Liuzhai in Qian, can shorten the journey by 300 li. It has a great relationship with the passenger and cargo traffic between Qian province and Haikou. From the perspective of the interests of the Gui, Yue, and San provinces, its importance cannot be compared to the Danchi Road. Therefore, it is planned to build the Limeng Road in the second year, and then build this line in the third year.

Fourth Year Construction Routes

(1) Complete the Hewu Road. This road starts from Hexian city, passing through Shuizhutang, Meihua, Malianjie, Xindu city, to Shatou, and then from Shatou via Shiqiao Fengmen Gorge to Shanxin, and reaching Dali River of Cangwu. It is 360 li long. Except for the section from Shanxin to Dalikou, which has already been completed, the roadbed of the 120 li section from Jiaxian city to Xindu city has also been built. However, the 150 li section from Huanghua in Xindu to Shanxin in Cangwu has not been constructed with roadbeds or culverts. The relationship between this road and the culture, economy, politics, and military of the Gui and Wu areas is as important as the Limeng Road, and it will be of considerable help to the development of the Fuhezhong mining area. Therefore, after the Jiuda Road is built in the third year, this line will continue to be completed.

(2) Build the Wuhuang Road. This road starts from Wuxuan city and ends at Dahuanjiang, which belongs to Guiping county. The section from Wuxuan to Xinluju is relatively flat. The section from Xinluqiao to Sanliwei is mostly mountainous. The section from Sanliwei via Sanjiangba to Dahongchongkou in Dongxiang also mostly runs along the mountainside. The section from Dahongchongkou to Hualeicun is quite rugged. The section from Hualeicun to Sanjiangwei is all gravel. In Sanjiangwei to Xinxu, there is a stone cliff gorge that can only accommodate one person walking, which is quite dangerous. From here, you will reach the Dahuanjiang River Estuary. The entire road is 200 li long. After the completion of this road, the Liuzhou area highway can be directly connected to the big river. Crossing the river south from Dahuanjiang can also be connected to the main line of the Wuzhou area highway.
